Welcome to Abella 2.0.7-dev. 
Abella < Kind nat Type.


Abella < Import "../../lib/nat".
Importing from "../../lib/nat".


Abella < Kind atm Type.


Abella < Type a, b, c, d, e, f atm.


Abella < Type atom, natom atm -> o.


Abella < Type tens, par o -> o -> o.


Abella < Type one, bot o.


Abella < Type bang, qm o -> o.


Abella < Define is_fm : o -> prop by 
is_fm (atom A);
is_fm (natom A);
is_fm (tens A B) := is_fm A /\ is_fm B;
is_fm (par A B) := is_fm A /\ is_fm B;
is_fm one;
is_fm bot;
is_fm (bang A) := is_fm A;
is_fm (qm A) := is_fm A.


Abella < Define dual : o -> o -> prop by 
dual (atom A) (natom A);
dual (tens A B) (par AA BB) := dual A AA /\ dual B BB;
dual one bot;
dual (bang A) (qm AA) := dual A AA.


Abella < Theorem dual_is : 
forall A B, dual A B -> is_fm A /\ is_fm B.



============================
 forall A B, dual A B -> is_fm A /\ is_fm B

dual_is < induction on 1.


IH : forall A B, dual A B * -> is_fm A /\ is_fm B
============================
 forall A B, dual A B @ -> is_fm A /\ is_fm B

dual_is < intros.


Variables: A B
IH : forall A B, dual A B * -> is_fm A /\ is_fm B
H1 : dual A B @
============================
 is_fm A /\ is_fm B

dual_is < case H1.

Subgoal 1:

Variables: A1
IH : forall A B, dual A B * -> is_fm A /\ is_fm B
============================
 is_fm (atom A1) /\ is_fm (natom A1)

Subgoal 2 is:
 is_fm (tens A1 B1) /\ is_fm (par AA BB)

Subgoal 3 is:
 is_fm one /\ is_fm bot

Subgoal 4 is:
 is_fm (bang A1) /\ is_fm (qm AA)

dual_is < search.

Subgoal 2:

Variables: BB AA B1 A1
IH : forall A B, dual A B * -> is_fm A /\ is_fm B
H2 : dual A1 AA *
H3 : dual B1 BB *
============================
 is_fm (tens A1 B1) /\ is_fm (par AA BB)

Subgoal 3 is:
 is_fm one /\ is_fm bot

Subgoal 4 is:
 is_fm (bang A1) /\ is_fm (qm AA)

dual_is < apply IH to *H2.

Subgoal 2:

Variables: BB AA B1 A1
IH : forall A B, dual A B * -> is_fm A /\ is_fm B
H3 : dual B1 BB *
H4 : is_fm A1
H5 : is_fm AA
============================
 is_fm (tens A1 B1) /\ is_fm (par AA BB)

Subgoal 3 is:
 is_fm one /\ is_fm bot

Subgoal 4 is:
 is_fm (bang A1) /\ is_fm (qm AA)

dual_is < apply IH to *H3.

Subgoal 2:

Variables: BB AA B1 A1
IH : forall A B, dual A B * -> is_fm A /\ is_fm B
H4 : is_fm A1
H5 : is_fm AA
H6 : is_fm B1
H7 : is_fm BB
============================
 is_fm (tens A1 B1) /\ is_fm (par AA BB)

Subgoal 3 is:
 is_fm one /\ is_fm bot

Subgoal 4 is:
 is_fm (bang A1) /\ is_fm (qm AA)

dual_is < search.

Subgoal 3:

IH : forall A B, dual A B * -> is_fm A /\ is_fm B
============================

Subgoal 4 is:

H2 : dual A1 AA *
============================

Subgoal 4:

Variables: AA A1

Abella < Import "../../lib/merge" with is_o := is_fm.
Importing from "../../lib/merge".


Abella < Define mell : nat -> (list o) -> (list o) -> prop by 
mell (s X) QL L := is_nat X /\ is_list QL /\ (exists A, adj (natom A :: nil) (atom A) L);
mell (s X) QL L := exists A B LL, adj LL (tens A B) L /\
  (exists JJ KK, merge JJ KK LL /\ (exists J, adj JJ A J /\ mell X QL J) /\
       (exists K, adj KK B K /\ mell X QL K));
mell (s X) QL (one :: nil) := is_nat X /\ is_list QL;
mell (s X) QL L := exists A B LL, adj LL (par A B) L /\
  (exists J, adj LL A J /\ (exists K, adj J B K /\ mell X QL K));
mell (s X) QL L := exists LL, adj LL bot L /\ mell X QL LL;
mell (s X) QL (bang A :: nil) := mell X QL (A :: nil);
mell (s X) QL L := exists A LL, adj LL (qm A) L /\ (exists QK, adj QL A QK /\ mell X QK LL);
mell (s X) QL L := exists A QK, adj QK A QL /\ (exists J, adj L A J /\ mell X QL J).


Abella < Theorem mell_is : 
forall X QL L, mell X QL L -> is_nat X /\ is_list QL /\ is_list L.



============================
 forall X QL L, mell X QL L -> is_nat X /\ is_list QL /\ is_list L

Abella < Theorem mell_weaken_height : 
forall X Y QL L, mell X QL L -> leq X Y -> mell Y QL L.



============================
 forall X Y QL L, mell X QL L -> leq X Y -> mell Y QL L

mell_weaken_height < induction on 1.


IH : forall X Y QL L, mell X QL L * -> leq X Y -> mell Y QL L
============================
 forall X Y QL L, mell X QL L @ -> leq X Y -> mell Y QL L

mell_weaken_height < intros.


Variables: X Y QL L
IH : forall X Y QL L, mell X QL L * -> leq X Y -> mell Y QL L

H2 : leq X Y
============================

Abella < Theorem mell_equalize_height : 
forall X QK K Y QL L, mell X QK K -> mell Y QL L ->
  (exists Z, mell Z QK K /\ mell Z QL L).



============================
 forall X QK K Y QL L, mell X QK K -> mell Y QL L ->
   (exists Z, mell Z QK K /\ mell Z QL L)

mell_equalize_height < intros.


Variables: X QK K Y QL L
H1 : mell X QK K
H2 : mell Y QL L
============================
 exists Z, mell Z QK K /\ mell Z QL L

mell_equalize_height < apply mell_is to H1.


Variables: X QK K Y QL L
H1 : mell X QK K
H2 : mell Y QL L
H3 : is_nat X
H4 : is_list QK
H5 : is_list K
============================
 exists Z, mell Z QK K /\ mell Z QL L

mell_equalize_height < apply mell_is to H2.

H1 : mell X QK K
H2 : mell Y QL L
H3 : is_nat X
H4 : is_list QK
H5 : is_list K
H6 : is_nat Y
H7 : is_list QL
H8 : is_list L
============================
 exists Z, mell Z QK K /\ mell Z QL L

mell_equalize_height < apply max_exists to H3 H6.

H5 : is_list K

H9 : max X Y Z
============================
 exists Z, mell Z QK K /\ mell Z QL L

mell_equalize_height < apply max_leq to H9.


Variables: X QK K Y QL L Z
H1 : mell X QK K
H2 : mell Y QL L

============================
 exists Z, mell Z QK K /\ mell Z QL L

mell_equalize_height < apply mell_weaken_height to H1 H10.

Proof completed.

Abella < Theorem bot_inv : 
forall X QL J L, mell X QL L -> adj J bot L -> mell X QL J.



============================
 forall X QL J L, mell X QL L -> adj J bot L -> mell X QL J

bot_inv < induction on 1.


IH : forall X QL J L, mell X QL L * -> adj J bot L -> mell X QL J
============================
 forall X QL J L, mell X QL L @ -> adj J bot L -> mell X QL J

bot_inv < intros.

Proof completed.

Abella < Theorem par_inv : 
forall A B X QL L J KA KAB, mell X QL L -> adj J (par A B) L -> adj J A KA ->
  adj KA B KAB -> mell X QL KAB.



============================
 forall A B X QL L J KA KAB, mell X QL L -> adj J (par A B) L ->
   adj J A KA -> adj KA B KAB -> mell X QL KAB

par_inv < induction on 1.


IH : forall A B X QL L J KA KAB, mell X QL L * -> adj J (par A B) L ->
       adj J A KA -> adj KA B KAB -> mell X QL KAB
============================
 forall A B X QL L J KA KAB, mell X QL L @ -> adj J (par A B) L ->
   adj J A KA -> adj KA B KAB -> mell X QL KAB

par_inv < intros.


Variables: A B X QL L J KA KAB
IH : forall A B X QL L J KA KAB, mell X QL L * -> adj J (par A B) L ->
       adj J A KA -> adj KA B KAB -> mell X QL KAB
H1 : mell X QL L @
H2 : adj J (par A B) L
H3 : adj J A KA
H4 : adj KA B KAB
============================
 mell X QL KAB

Proof completed.

Abella < Theorem qm_inv : 
forall A X QL L J QK, mell X QL L -> adj J (qm A) L -> adj QL A QK ->
  mell X QK J.



============================
 forall A X QL L J QK, mell X QL L -> adj J (qm A) L -> adj QL A QK ->
   mell X QK J

qm_inv < induction on 1.


IH : forall A X QL L J QK, mell X QL L * -> adj J (qm A) L -> adj QL A QK ->
       mell X QK J
============================
 forall A X QL L J QK, mell X QL L @ -> adj J (qm A) L -> adj QL A QK ->
   mell X QK J

qm_inv < intros.


Variables: A X QL L J QK
IH : forall A X QL L J QK, mell X QL L * -> adj J (qm A) L -> adj QL A QK ->
       mell X QK J
H1 : mell X QL L @
H2 : adj J (qm A) L
H3 : adj QL A QK
============================
 mell X QK J

qm_inv < case H1.

Subgoal 1:

Variables: A QL L J QK A1 X1
IH : forall A X QL L J QK, mell X QL L * -> adj J (qm A) L -> adj QL A QK ->
       mell X QK J
H2 : adj J (qm A) L
H3 : adj QL A QK
H4 : is_nat X1
H5 : is_list QL
H6 : adj (natom A1 :: nil) (atom A1) L
============================
 mell (s X1) QK J

Subgoal 2 is:
 mell (s X1) QK J

Subgoal 3 is:
 mell (s X1) QK J

Subgoal 4 is:
 mell (s X1) QK J

Subgoal 5 is:
 mell (s X1) QK J

Subgoal 6 is:
 mell (s X1) QK J

Subgoal 7 is:
 mell (s X1) QK J

Subgoal 8 is:
 mell (s X1) QK J

qm_inv < case H6.

Subgoal 1.1:

Variables: A QL J QK A1 X1
IH : forall A X QL L J QK, mell X QL L * -> adj J (qm A) L -> adj QL A QK ->
       mell X QK J

Abella < Kind weight Type.


Abella < Type heavy, light weight.


Abella < Define is_weight : weight -> prop by 
is_weight light;
is_weight heavy := is_weight light.


Abella < Theorem $cut_admit : 
forall A B X W, dual A B -> is_nat X -> is_weight W -> W = light /\
  (forall JJ J KK K QL Y LL, adj JJ A J -> mell X QL J -> adj KK B K ->
       mell Y QL K -> merge JJ KK LL -> (exists Z, mell Z QL LL)) \/
  W =
heavy /\
  (forall QL QQ K Y, mell X QL (A :: nil) -> adj QL B QQ -> mell Y QQ K ->
       (exists Z, mell Z QL K)).

Abella < Theorem cut_admit_linear : 
forall A B X Y JJ J KK K QL LL, dual A B -> adj JJ A J -> mell X QL J ->
  adj KK B K -> mell Y QL K -> merge JJ KK LL -> (exists Z, mell Z QL LL).



============================
 forall A B X Y JJ J KK K QL LL, dual A B -> adj JJ A J -> mell X QL J ->
   adj KK B K -> mell Y QL K -> merge JJ KK LL -> (exists Z, mell Z QL LL)

cut_admit_linear < intros.

H1 : dual A B
H2 : adj JJ A J
H3 : mell X QL J
H4 : adj KK B K
H5 : mell Y QL K
H6 : merge JJ KK LL
============================
 exists Z, mell Z QL LL

H7 : is_nat X
H8 : is_list QL
H9 : is_list J
============================
 exists Z, mell Z QL LL

cut_admit_linear < apply $cut_admit to H1 H7 _ with W = light.

        (forall JJ J KK K QL Y LL, adj JJ A J -> mell X QL J -> adj KK B K ->
             mell Y QL K -> merge JJ KK LL -> (exists Z, mell Z QL LL)) \/
        light =
      heavy /\
        (forall QL QQ K Y, mell X QL (A :: nil) -> adj QL B QQ ->
             mell Y QQ K -> (exists Z, mell Z QL K))
